    <script>
  function custom_sort(a, b) {
    return new Date(a.date).getTime() - new Date(b.date).getTime();
}
  function filterArrByDate(arr, fromDate, toDate){
   return arr.filter(function(d) {var time = new Date(d.name.split(" ")[1].replaceAll("-", "/")).getTime();
                             return (fromDate < time && time < toDate);
                            }); 
  }

  document.getElementById("block-yui_3_17_2_1_1696891017171_12275").style.display = "none";
   	var days = 7; // Days you want to subtract
    var fromDate = new Date((new Date()).getTime() - (1 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
    var toDate = new Date(fromDate.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
  if(screen.width <= 400) {
  document.getElementById("divR").style.display = "block" /* show it on small screens */
  document.getElementById("divNR").style.display = "none"
}
else if(screen.width > 400) {
  document.getElementById("divR").style.display = "none" /* show it on big screens */
  document.getElementById("divNR").style.display = "block"
}
  // Get North Region restaurants data
  axios.get('https://mobileapp.asucla.ucla.edu:3004/api/property/UCLA%20Restaurants%20-				%20North%20Campus').then(function (Response){
    const ResponseData = Response.data;
   	if (ResponseData.length > 0) {
		let temp = ""; 
      	let responsive = "";
		for(let i=0; i<ResponseData.length; i++){
          temp += "<tr>";
          temp += "<td>" + "<b>" + ResponseData[i].name + "</b>" + 
            "<br/>" + ResponseData[i].location + "<br/>"+ "<br/>"+
            ResponseData[i].phoneNumber +"</td>";
          responsive += "<div class='containerR bg-blue'><b>" + ResponseData[i].name + "</b>" + "<br/>" +ResponseData[i].location + "<br/>"+ ResponseData[i].phoneNumber +"</div>";
          	ResponseData[i].availability.sort(custom_sort);
          ResponseData[i].availability = filterArrByDate(ResponseData[i].availability, fromDate, toDate);
           	for(let j=0; j< ResponseData[i].availability.length; j++){
       			temp += "<td>" + ResponseData[i].availability[j].value + "</td>";
              	responsive+="<div class='containerRI'><div><b>" + (ResponseData[0].availability[j].name).replaceAll('-','/').toUpperCase() + ": </b></div><div>" + ResponseData[i].availability[j].value + "</div></div>"
       		}
        }
       let head = "<tr><th>Location</th>";
       let availability = ResponseData[0].availability;
 	   for(let j=0; j< availability.length; j++){
        head+= "<th>"+ (availability[j].name).replaceAll('-','/') +"</th>";      
       }
      head+="</tr>";
      document.getElementById('ncR').innerHTML = responsive;
      document.getElementById('northHeadData').innerHTML = head;
      document.getElementById('northBodyData').innerHTML = temp;
      }
	})

<script>
   window.onscroll = function() {scrollFunction()};

   function scrollFunction() {
      if (document.body.scrollTop > 20 || document.documentElement.scrollTop > 20)
      {
         document.getElementById("myBtn").style.display = "block";
      } else {
         document.getElementById("myBtn").style.display = "none";
      }
   }

   function topFunction() {
      $('html,body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 0);
   }
